<h1 _ngcontent-pro-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.data.rdb (关系型数据库)"> @ohos.data.rdb (关系型数据库) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>关系型数据库（Relational Database，RDB）是一种基于关系模型来管理数据的数据库。关系型数据库基于SQLite组件提供了一套完整的对本地数据库进行管理的机制，对外提供了一系列的增、删、改、查等接口，也可以直接运行用户输入的SQL语句来满足复杂的场景需要。不支持Worker线程。</p>    <p>该模块提供以下关系型数据库相关的常用功能：</p>    <ul>     <li><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-data-rdb#rdbpredicates">RdbPredicates</a>：数据库中用来代表数据实体的性质、特征或者数据实体之间关系的词项，主要用来定义数据库的操作条件。</li>     <li><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-data-rdb#rdbstore">RdbStore</a>：提供管理关系数据库（RDB）方法的接口。</li>    </ul>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <ul>       <li>        <p>本模块首批接口从API version 7开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p></li>       <li>        <p>从API version 9开始，该接口不再维护，推荐使用新接口<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-data-relationalstore">@ohos.data.relationalStore</a>。</p></li>      </ul>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-pro-c106=""  <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1841px;">     <h2 id="data_rdbgetrdbstore" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">data_rdb.getRdbStore<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="data_rdbgetrdbstore" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getRdbStore(context: Context, config: StoreConfig, version: number, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;RdbStore&gt;): void</p>     <p>获得一个相关的RdbStore，操作关系型数据库，用户可以根据自己的需求配置RdbStore的参数，然后通过RdbStore调用相关接口可以执行相关的数据操作，使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.DistributedDataManager.RelationalStore.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">context</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Context</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>应用的上下文。</p>          <p>FA模型的应用Context定义见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inner-app-context">Context</a>。</p>          <p>Stage模型的应用Context定义见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inner-app-context">Context</a>。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">config</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-data-rdb#storeconfig">StoreConfig</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">与此RDB存储相关的数据库配置。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">version</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>数据库版本。</p>          <p>目前暂不支持通过version自动识别数据库升级降级操作，只能由开发者自行维护。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-data-rdb#rdbstore">RdbStore</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定callback回调函数，返回RdbStore对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <p>FA模型示例：</p>     <div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">data_rdb.getRdbStore<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="data_rdbgetrdbstore-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getRdbStore(context: Context, config: StoreConfig, version: number): Promise&lt;RdbStore&gt;</p>     <p>获得一个相关的RdbStore，操作关系型数据库，用户可以根据自己的需求配置RdbStore的参数，然后通过RdbStore调用相关接口可以执行相关的数据操作，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.DistributedDataManager.RelationalStore.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">context</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Context</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>应用的上下文。</p>          <p>FA模型的应用Context定义见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inner-app-context">Context</a>。</p>          <p>Stage模型的应用Context定义见<a class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">与此RDB存储相关的数据库配置。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">version</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>数据库版本。</p>          <p>目前暂不支持通过version自动识别数据库升级降级操作，只能由开发者自行维护。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>offsetAs(rowOffset: number): RdbPredicates</p>     <p>配置RdbPredicates以指定返回结果的起始位置。需要同步调用limitAs接口指定查询数量，否则将无查询结果。如需查询指定偏移位置后的所有行，limitAs接口调用需传参数-1。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.DistributedDataManager.RelationalStore.Core</p> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">RdbStore<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="rdbstore" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>提供管理关系数据库（RDB）方法的接口。</p>     <p>在使用以下相关接口前，请使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-data-rdb#executesql8">executeSql</a>接口初始化数据库表结构和相关数据。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1280px;">     <h3 id="insert" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">insert<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="insert" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>insert(table: string, values: ValuesBucket, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;number&gt;):void</p>     <p>向目标表中插入一行数据，使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.DistributedDataManager.RelationalStore.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">table</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的目标表名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">values</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-data-rdb#valuesbucket">ValuesBucket</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">表示要插入到表中的数据行。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;number&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定callback回调函数。如果操作成功，返回行ID；否则返回-1。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-pro-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>off(event:'dataChange', type: SubscribeType, observer: Callback&lt;Array&lt;string&gt;&gt;): void</p>     <p>从数据库中删除指定类型的指定观察者，使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.DistributedDataManager.RelationalStore.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table> width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">event</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td
